     <p> The skeleton of a huge dragon is fossilised in one of the cliff faces here. Its wings are spread as if it was about to fly to the clouds one last time. </p>   <p> <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll('8JeW9F0B');"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a> Several caravans are circling a large camp fire on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail. The ghost now controls the body but doesn't deprive the target of awareness. The ghost can't be targeted by any attack, spell, or other effect, except ones that turn undead, and it retains its alignment, Intelligence, Wisdom, Charisma, and immunity to being <strong>charmed</strong> and <strong>frightened</strong>.       <p> The White Wyverns syndicate are conspiring to assassinate the ruler of the realm. </p>  <p> The syndicates usual gathering venue is <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/X1ruZaji"><strong>"The Flaming Torch Lodge"</strong></a> in <strong>Balaal</strong> </p> 
      <p> The syndicate leader is a <strong>Latilde Ormonde</strong>, a level 10 Elf Rogue.  She has braided red hair, cold dark eyes and long, pointy ears (<em>Nervous</em>). <small>In the pocket: <strong>3 cp</strong>, <strong>an empty vial</strong> and <strong>a key</strong>.</small>
